			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of cities by longitude</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><p>The following is a <b>list of cities by longitude</b>. Both the <a href="/wiki/Latitude" title="Latitude">latitude</a> and <a href="/wiki/Longitude" title="Longitude">longitude</a> are shown for the following <a href="/wiki/City" title="City">cities</a>, which are sorted by longitude from the west of the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Meridian" title="Prime Meridian" class="mw-redirect">Prime Meridian</a> to the east. Each heading should be considered the exact value. For example, 10°E corresponds to exactly 10°00′00.00″E and everything further west should be above this heading while everything further east should be below this heading.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="90.C2.B0W"><a href="/wiki/90th_meridian_west" title="90th meridian west">90°W</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_cities_by_longitude&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 90°W">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable sortable jquery-tablesorter">
<thead><tr>
